function info($str) { echo "INFO: $str\n"; }
function warn($str) { echo "WARNING: $str\n"; }
function err($str) { die("FATAL ERROR: $str\n"); }

@set_time_limit(0);

	err('This update can only be applied to OIDplus version 2.0.0.624!');
}

if (version_compare(PHP_VERSION, '7.0.0') < 0) {
	err('You need PHP Version 7.0 to update to this version');
}

if (!is_file('doc/config_values.txt')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: doc/config_values.txt');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('doc/config_values.txt')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): doc/config_values.txt');
	} else if (sha1_file('doc/config_values.txt') != 'ec531cabd468f87a022f0866ec4458e396f02b87') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): doc/config_values.txt');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('doc/config_values.txt', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of doc/config_values.txt');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('doc/config_values.txt') !== 'ec531cabd468f87a022f0866ec4458e396f02b87') {
		if (@sha1_file('doc/config_values.txt') !== 'afd28ade4c2640d50c0129f42f21a40748c562f5') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: doc/config_values.txt');
			$tmp = pathinfo('doc/config_values.txt');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('doc/config_values.txt')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('doc/config_values.txt', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('doc/config_values.txt') !== 'ec531cabd468f87a022f0866ec4458e396f02b87') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): doc/config_values.txt');
		}
	}
}

}
if (!is_file('doc/ldap_installation.txt')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: doc/ldap_installation.txt');
	writefile_2();
	if (!is_file('doc/ldap_installation.txt')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): doc/ldap_installation.txt');
	} else if (sha1_file('doc/ldap_installation.txt') != '9f348807031f432a6f0bd311218cd9e4714f27f4') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): doc/ldap_installation.txt');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('doc/ldap_installation.txt', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of doc/ldap_installation.txt');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('doc/ldap_installation.txt') !== '9f348807031f432a6f0bd311218cd9e4714f27f4') {
		if (@sha1_file('doc/ldap_installation.txt') !== 'a34c8d95352d97935f46618599af1b29b7b5ad09') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: doc/ldap_installation.txt');
			$tmp = pathinfo('doc/ldap_installation.txt');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('doc/ldap_installation.txt')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('doc/ldap_installation.txt', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('doc/ldap_installation.txt') !== '9f348807031f432a6f0bd311218cd9e4714f27f4') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): doc/ldap_installation.txt');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('includes/functions.inc.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/functions.inc.php');
	writefile_3();
	if (!is_file('includes/functions.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/functions.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/functions.inc.php') != '97953be9c20c55837f2396d13c73c9d9a379eaf3') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/functions.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/functions.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/functions.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/functions.inc.php') !== '97953be9c20c55837f2396d13c73c9d9a379eaf3') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/functions.inc.php') !== 'fc7f2909bca7f6f6e233646219dfbd66b6d82dad') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/functions.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/functions.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/functions.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/functions.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/functions.inc.php') !== '97953be9c20c55837f2396d13c73c9d9a379eaf3') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/functions.inc.php');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	writefile_4();
	if (!is_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') != '2cfb4cb13fa74befa0730fe5a3528b3c3392bf09') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '2cfb4cb13fa74befa0730fe5a3528b3c3392bf09') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '7e4bc205c7725663f2a7a3a661e1013c316c14f7') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_4();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '2cfb4cb13fa74befa0730fe5a3528b3c3392bf09') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
		}
	}
}
